| 0:02:11| or defer his or her opening remarks and allow any opposition to speak first.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=131)|
| 0:02:17| The applicant and those in support of the applicant| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=137)|
| 0:02:19| will be given a total of five minutes to speak.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=139)|
| 0:02:23| I will then ask for other comments from the floor.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=143)|
| 0:02:26| The opposition will also be given a total of five minutes to speak.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=146)|
| 0:02:30| If either side wishes to have an opportunity for rebuttal,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=150)|
| 0:02:34| you'll need to reserve time from your allotted five minutes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=154)|

| 0:46:50| and the community reviews, again, has already been vetted on the design side.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2810)|
| 0:46:54| But an applicant is obligated to submit a site plan and elevation drawings.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2814)|
| 0:47:00| We have a staff pre-review process, so we review the site plan with city codes, zoning,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2820)|
| 0:47:05| and engineering staff to ensure that it meets the relevant codes, identify any issues that they run into in permitting.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2825)|
| 0:47:12| We take a quick look at the principal use standards for if they were townhouses or duplexes,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2832)|
| 0:47:18| whatever form of house it would be.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2838)|
| 0:47:20| And then we provide a staff report of how it meets the infill housing design guidelines.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2840)|
| 0:47:25| The Design Review Board would then review and approve, approve with conditions, or deny.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2845)|
| 0:47:31| There's a 14-day appeal period, and that would be the infill housing process side of it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2851)|
| 0:47:38| And then during the special use process, we would ask for similar documents, site plan elevations,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2858)|
| 0:47:45| circulation, off-street parking.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2865)|
| 0:47:47| We have an interagency review where we review the site plan with engineering and other relevant departments.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2867)|
| 0:47:56| And we are reviewing it for compatibility with the surrounding neighborhood,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2876)|
| 0:48:02| consistency with adopted plans, considering potential negative impacts.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2882)|
| 0:48:09| And that goes before the planning commission.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2889)|
| 0:48:11| We post signs in advance of the planning commission meeting,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2891)|
| 0:48:14| so there is community input in the special use review.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2894)|
| 0:48:21| And in that process, if, say, there was feedback about dumpster locations or the stepping of these,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2901)|
| 0:48:33| and I know that the dumpster mentioned is on an adjacent property,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2913)|
| 0:48:36| but maybe the developer could combine those and kind of offer something, some form of relief to the neighbors.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2916)|
| 0:48:48| But if there were comments about that, would that come up in the DRB approval process of those layouts and things?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2928)|
| 0:48:56| Yes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-230810?start=2936)|
